Montana   Real Recognize Real    Outro DuFlocka Rant          Background   Juaquin James Malphurs better known as Waka Flocka Flame or simply Waka Flocka is the original pioneer of the modern day trap scene that is so prevalent around the United States Born in New York but growing up in Riverdale Georgia Waka Flocka set the underground trap world ablaze with his hit single O Lets Do It in  It wasnt until  with the release of the  club banger Hard in the Paint that mainstream audiences began to notice Waka  more single followed in late  No Hands feat Roscoe Dash and Wale creating an unprecedented buzz for the underground trap artist who was being  groomed and repped by non other than the legends himself Gucci Mane Waka Flocka proceeds to drop in October of  one of the greatest debuts for a hiphop artist of the new decade and in my opinion a certified classic in modern day hiphop Flockaveli almost entirely produced by Lex Luger becomes a staple and blueprint in the modern day trap scene Fast foward to  after slew of mixtapes from Salute Me or Shoot Me series to his sophomore album Triple F Life Friends Fans  Family Waka continues his dominance in the trap scene and without anybody noticing proceeds to drop a BLASSIC mixtape by the name of Duflocka Rant  hosted by TRAPAHOLICS  DJ ACE released    Review   the lyrics posted will be my favorite lyrics from the song    DuFlocka Rant character Percy Jackson He urges us to close the book immediately Percy Jackson is a  year old boy who attends Yancy Academy a private school for troubled kids His life changes dramatically during a field trip to the Metropolitan Museum of Art Previous field trips did not go well for Percy at his previous schools accidents having occurred on every trip On this trip two chaperones led the group of students Mr Brunner the Latin teacher and Percys favorite and Mrs Dodds the math teacher Percys only friend Grover is on the trip as well   After a disagreement with his school bully Nancy Bobofit at the water fountain Percy is falsely accused of pushing her when she suddenly finds herself soaked in the ankle deep water Mrs Dodds leads Percy away from the group demanding a confession from him as she transforms into a horrid creature with bat wings and yellow fangs Mr Brunner suddenly appears and tosses Percy a ballpoint pen that turns into a bronze sword Percy swings the sword as the monster lunges at him and it turns to dust Dazed by this experience Percy finds that when he returns to the group no one remembers Mrs Dodds   Chapter  Three Old Ladies Knit the Socks of Death  No one recalls that Mrs Dodds was ever at the school or even existed which convinces Percy something else is going on Frustrated that hes the only one that seems to know Percy continues to fight with Nancy neglect his grades and even disrespect a teacher which gets Percy expelled from Yancey Academy Percy decides the only final he will study for is Mr Brunners Latin final and he goes to Mr Brunners office for help Percy overhears a conversation between Mr Brunner and Grover about Percy and the incident with Mrs Dodds They talk about magical mist making all of the students and teachers forget Mrs Dodds and Grover explains how Percy may be the only one who can save them before the Summer Solstice  After the school year ends Percy confronts Grover on the bus about his conversation with Mr Brunner Grover reveals his role as Percys protector The bus breaks down and as they step off the bus Grover and Percy see three old women knitting huge socks and staring at Percy As Grover makes Percy promise to walk to Percys house together one of the old women cuts a string off the socks with a pair of large shears Grover reveals thanks to Percys prodding that the cut signifies that someones going to die  Chapter  Grover Unexpectedly Loses His Trousers  After the bus stops at the terminal Percy ditches Grover and walks home on his own Before readers enter the apartment Percy describes his mother Sally Jackson the best person Percy knows Shes had some unfortunate things happen in her life though she met Percys father which was the high point though he left on an ocean voyage before Percy was born about his day school etc as Percy eats candy brought home   Sally tells Percy that theyre going to Montauk Beach where shed met Percys father Gabe warns Percy as they leave not to scratch Gabes car and demands bean dip While at the beach Sally tells Percy about his father and Percy learns his father wanted to send Percy to a special camp That night as a hurricane thunders outside a knock on the door wakes Percy and Sally Grover is at the door saying he has been searching for Percy all night Sally is unfazed by Grovers presence and demands that Percy tells her everything that happened at the museum Percy explains and they run to the call Percy realizing that Grover has hooves for feet  Chapter  My Mom Teaches Me Bullfighting  While driving away from the storm Percy sees a large creature less monsters he attracts Based on Percys encounter with the three old women who Percy is told were The Fates Sally drives them to the camp Percys father wanted him to go to The car suddenly swerves leave without her or Grover as the creature is gaining on them   Sally and Percy finally manage to get Grover out of the car and head for the boundary Percy sees that the monster is half man half bull directions suddenly Percy does that as the bull charges which angers it The Minotaur grabbed Percys mother by the neck and she disappeared in a golden light Percy is furious which prompts him to attack the monster tearing off one of its horns and stabbing it in the ribs The creature bursts into dust and Percy drags Grover to safety collapsing on the porch of a farmhouse where a girl calls him the one  Chapter  I Play Pinochle with a Horse  Percy wakes up and passes out over and over being nursed back to health with some pudding tasting like buttered popcorn and the girl calling him the one last night feeding it to him and questioning him Percy wakes up to beautiful views of the camp unlike anything hed ever seen before Still mourning for his mother Percy reflects on the fight last night Grover shows up apologizing for Percys mothers death and failing his role as a keeper Percy does not blame Grover and they leave for the main part of Camp Half Blood Percy meets Mr D the reluctant camp director Chiron who Percy knew as Mr Brunner and Annabeth a Daughter of Athena who nursed him back to health  Percy joins Chiron Mr D and Grover in a game of Pinochle While playing the game they discuss the presence of Greek gods in the world revealing that Mr D is one himself Dionysus the god of wine put in charge of the camp as a punishment from his father Zeus Mr D and Grover leave so Percy and Chiron can talk privately Chiron and Percy discuss more about Mount Olympus and the gods Chiron informs Percy he will get settled into his cabin and then more information will come to him As Chiron goes to escort Percy he reveals his true form from his wheelchair a towering centaur  Chapter  I Become Supreme Lord of the Bathroom  Chiron now in centaur form gives Percy a tour of the camp 2	Hi rRepGirls   Business of Fashion released their Sustainability Index today and as the topic of sustainability comes up often in Rep vs Authentic debates I thought this would be interesting to the sub  Sustainable is a real buzzword right now in the same way as clean is with beauty I have numerous bones to pick with that term its thrown around a lot without much thought to what it means or the metrics you should evaluate it on Sustainability I think isnt a YesNo metric but a scale of how sustainable a brand is  BoH broke Sustainability down into  dimensions Transparency eg supply chains Emissions Water  Chemicals Materials Workers Rights and Waste  Luxury brands it discusses in order of BoHs ranking of sustainability   Kering score  which owns Gucci Yves Saint Laurent Bottega Veneta Balenciaga  PVH Corp score  which owns Tommy Hilfiger and Calvin Klein  Hermes score   LVMH score  which owns Celine Dior Fendi Givenchy Loewe Louis Vuitton Marc Jacobs  Richemont score  which owns Cartier and Chloe  Heres the full report and the main infographic for mobile users  Methodology   Methodology drafting Industry research and expert interviews inform the Index targets and metrics selected to measure progress The first draft of the methodology is devised  Sustainability Council consultations Our Sustainability Council reviews the methodology in full and partakes in consultations to refine the targets and metrics These are finalised and shared with the Council  Companies sent questionnaires Companies are notified of their inclusion in the project and are invited to complete a questionnaire of the metrics with publicly available evidence This is optional and not all companies participated  Research companies BoF researchers review each company and populate the questionnaire with evidence of relevant public disclosures to award preliminary points crosschecking and verifying evidence in responses submitted by the companies  Companies receive preliminary results and fact checks BoF researchers conduct quality assurance checks to ensure companies have been scored consistently and fairly against the metrics before sharing preliminary results with the companies along with any fact checks  Responses are reviewed Fact check responses and additional comments from the companies are reviewed and individual consultations with Council members over specific metrics take place  Data is compiled and finalised If a company provided additional information or disputed a finding this was reviewed and then either adjusted or not as considered appropriate  Final analysis and report prepared Data from each company is compiled into one complete dataset which is used to determine final scores and points of analysis BUSINESS OF FASHIONS SUSTAINABILITY INDEX AKA HOW SUSTAINABLE ARE LUXURY BRANDS REALLY

2	This post is Part One in a series intended to warn all unsuspecting Text RPGers who may happen upon a game called Achaea Dreams of Divine Lands before they make the grand mistake I did and drop a lot of cash into a supposedly free to play game ha thinking itd be easy to catch up with longer term players and open the door to limitless RP and combat potential  My plan is to cover topics like Why Retirement is a Scam The Legality of Loot Boxes and The Great Microtransaction Con along with delving into some little known history of the game its administration and the coverups the admin supposedly dont want anyone to know about  At some point Id also like to address issues of gender and sexuality in Achaea as well since there seems to be a lot of information readily available on how a game open to yearolds handles such situations Harassment forced textual relations and sexual fraternization with and amid the games administration are all possible future subjects  If this interests you read on  The first and perhaps most important thing that anyone needs to know about Achaea is that a lot of what its website promises is not legit A few of the more egregious claims are as follows lets delve a little into each one   Virtually all aspects of a city are run by playersOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Achaeas cities are run by players but this claim is actually advertising the potential for any player new to the game or old to take part in such organizational leadership The reality Ive uncovered is that Achaeas cities have been run since their inception by a handful of Garden think Divine Administration behind the scenes and in the sandbox of the world loyals and whales  One only needs to look at the oldest citizens of the game and its organizational hierarchy and history published on Achaeas own site and wiki to see evidence of this Since its inception in  organization after organization sprung up in the game with founders who worked closely with game administration to create their own little space and even new classes in the game  This of course makes total sense You build outward from charismatic and knowledgeable individuals in any organization But the foothold these and other players have in the game is somewhat staggering when compared to other text RPGs and visual MMOs  Since the formation and reformation in the case of Targossas of the main principalities each city has had what looks to be a revolving door of ruling council members But after discussing the game behind the scenes with longerterm players many of these individuals are just alts alterative characters of the same players who simply have a Godgranted stranglehold on RP leadership in the game  The same can be said for its Houses Many longplaying Achaeans I met and spoke with said that the sad reality is that whenever new players move in any of these organizations outside the vision of the games producers they are summarily dispensed from their roles and blacklisted to ensure they do not move back into leadership again That really turned me off especially when I witnessed some really questionable outcastings and enemyings in the city I belonged to in game that were almost entirely motivated by what appeared to be Divine influence  This hidden micromanagement of what is advertised to be an open world full of leadership potential is  therefore in my opinion one of the Achaeas dirtiest little secrets From Divine Administration metagaming with their former incharacter friends Divine are chosen from a pool of Achaeas current playerbase and rarely forego those friendships despite supposed rules against fraternization to Producers inhabiting denizen forms to outcast and blackball players stories some published in various forms online from players and former Divine persist and tell the tale of a much more controlled state of gameplay existence   Achaea has an elaborate system of highly fleshedout GodsOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Achaeas current Pantheon has  members Aegis Aurora Babel Deucalion Gaia Lorielan Neraeos Ourania Pandora Phaestus Prospero Sartan Scarlatti Tlalaiad Twilight Valnurana and Vastar  At one time Achaea had as many as as  divine the aforementioned divine plus Aeon Aeyr Agatheis Apollyon Artemis Balmet Caspian Clementius Daedalus Eris Glacius Hermes Indrani Kastalia Keresis Khalas Lucretius Lupus Matsuhama Maya Melantha Miramar Mithraea Oneiros Pandemonium Pentharian Raclawice Sarapis SElene Tarah Thoth and Varian  Although not all these Divine were actually played by volunteers what Achaea calls the behind the scenes workers who mostly are required to work  hours a week for the opportunity to play these roles without any compensation the majority were A few were historical characters in the games lore though and some were solely eventdriven roles abandoned after happenstance ingame  Today the majority of these Divine rosters are either dead or missing Out of the  currently existing members of the games fleshed out Pantheon yes well give them that point  each God has deepdeveloped lore that is truly top notch although that all changes each time a new divine volunteer takes up one of the roles as evidenced from history ingame and on their own wiki and website only Lorielan who is rumoured to be played by the games main producer is actually awake and active at this time  and shes not been seen since June  when she wrestled a portion of a city away from another Divines unwanted control a roleplay event  Going down the list I approximate this as the current level of actual Divine activity   Aegis left Achaea amid the COVID pandemic  Aurora has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Babel has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Deucalion has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Gaia has been reincarnated multiple times and recently announced her inactivity  Neraeos is inactive  Ourania is inactive  Pandora is rumoured to be inactive following her most recent ingame series of events  Phaestus works solely behind the scenes now when hes not creating oneoff events for his ingame friends and loyals  Prospero is inactive  Sartan is inactive  Scarlatti is inactive It is rumoured that a player once paid thousands of dollars to bypass all Celani divine admin training protocol and played the role into the murky mudsexed ground  Tlalaiad is active but holds a behind the scenes role mainly  Twilight has been reincarnated multiple times and his most recent incarnation is inactive after moving over to become the producer of Iron Realm Entertainments Aetolia  Valnurana has been inactive before her reallife spouse Tecton left the main producers role in  to champion IREs failed Starmourn venture  Vastar has been reincarnated multiple times and is currently inactive  Some sightings of these Gods inrealm are purportedly the result of Producers assuming their roles for eventbased shenanigans leaving the serious roleplay value of their highly fleshedout Gods in question   Smaller tighter friendlier communitiesOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be ALMOST ENTIRELY FALSE  Achaea is mainly comprised of cliques of people Although these are definitely smaller and tighter communities than found in many RPG and MMO games they are not necessarily friendlier despite the advertisement to the contrary  Just like in high school these groups of players breed an atmosphere of exclusivity and toxicity Rather than the friendly highly collaborative open world of possibilities that Achaea advertises not everyone has equal input in most instances And like most cliques they are darn hard to enter and become a valued part of the group  Instead there are Mean Girls in every city and organization in the game who use players desire to fit in and belong to their advantage There are typically  dominant persons in every organization who are spreading gossip based on their personal past with others even to the point of outing players who have retired Achaeas system of starting over on a new anonymous character Discord plays a big role in this  Anyone who has ever served as a manager knows that good directors or game producers in this game do not tolerate cliques and instead foster community and inclusiveness with healthy competition to help spur innovation and engagement Sadly we do not find such leaders in Achaea at present  Management openly sanctions fraternization allowing divine to befriend and communicate with players on their official discord Ive been invited and participated in a conversation with a Divine myself there already work ingame to endorse one group of people or individual players over others and perpetuate an illusion of a safe roleplay environment while subtly and sometimes quite openly criticizing certain players in various venues particularly Discord who dont get on board with their intended gameplay   The Nexus Client  the best way to play AchaeaOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  After starting out on a few newbie characters it quickly became apparent that the top combatants in the game do not utilize Achaeas Nexus Client Most in my experience utilize Mudlet and a package created by one of Achaeas own players that is known as AK affliction tracking  I liked Nexus as a newbie myself but I did find it jarring in the respect that this is a text game and the main draw of Nexus is its visual components There is just a real disconnection here for me  Although I cannot go into real depth about this particular claim a poll of a random  players throughout the months of September through November found that  were using a client other than Nexus There has to be a reason for this and I would love to hear your opinions on it and incorporate them into a future post in this series   The freedom of choice and possibilities in the game are endlessOUR TRUTH DETECTOR found this claim to be SOMEWHAT FALSE  Players are largely boxed in by their choices in Achaea Choose a class that is factional and youre locked into a particular city Divine followers face a similar hazard Make a wrong move and forget about it You lose all your friends your family may disown you and youll likely be mischaracterized to the hilt to justify the harsh repercussions  The possibilities of what can be are largely overshadowed by three things   Longterm players who will quote game lore and supposed canon at you and tell you that youre wrong and cannot possibly RP things  Cliques of players who control the various organizations and castigate anyone who steps outside the boundaries of the roleplay they deem to be acceptable  Divine producers who are unwilling to allow anyone to intentionally or unintentionally circumvent their intended roleplay vision for the realm  Another thing that I came across in this text RPG is the existence of a subclass of player who are basically blacklisted from joining any organization At first I thought this to be a small group of RPGers who had simply done some things so nefarious that they were cast out from the communitys inner circles yet were not bad enough to be shrubbed Achaeas version of a ban however upon inspection it seems that personal bias against individual players is what is really at work which is just sad because most of these individuals have invested thousands of reallife dollars in their characters    To sum things up never in my  years of playing RPGs and MMOs have I run across a more closed and limited gaming world than Achaea Thats just my opinion though and I would love to hear yours as well as ideas for new topics in this series of posts Ill be trying to release at least one a week starting in the new year Acheaa Dream of Divine Scams  Part I

4	This is not a drill  After years of continued inaction and hollow promises  is shaping to be the year that kicks off decisive regulatory action regarding sustainability across the fashion industry  France of course started the year with a bang by introducing new mandates for fashions largest brands requiring them to provide indepth information regarding material composition manufacturing location and other environmental characteristics linked to their products  The law applies to brands that sell more than  items annually in France and generate revenue above  million from domestic sales  New York and California have also passed recent bans on the toxic chemicals commonly used in waterproof outerwear The proposed New York Fashion Act which combines exacting due diligence and transparency requirements could also expose brands to penalties worth up to  percent of global revenue if passed  This flurry of regulatory action taking shape across the EU and the US is set to end years of inaction over the fashion industrys environmental and social footprint  Obviously this is great news So whats the bad news Simply put brands are not ready for these changes to take effect  Compliance with these new regulations will be challenging to measure and brands will have the devils job of uncovering how much impact production and operations genuinely have on the environment especially on a perproduct basis  While many of you may be unsympathetic toward brands in this scenario consider this quick fact A lack of readiness means brands are highly likely to delay and request grace periods as they scramble to obtain the information and establish the systems needed to document each products impact  Some proposed regulations will likely take years to pass fully Fortunately others  like Frances newest law  will require companies to act now  Regardless the risk of deteriorating ones brand image or facing potential fineslegal action has prominent brands like LVMH taking action now For example their recent partnership with the data management platform Fairly Made was established purely to gather and keep track of the information it needs to comply with these new regulations   will be an interesting and exciting year for the sustainable fashion movement to say the least  TLDR As exacting laws on transparency and ethical practices grow nearer brands are scrambling to pick up the pieces to avoid potential legal action and monetary andor reputational losses The action itself is welcome news but the true change will likely take some time to manifest as brands will need time to establish the systems and processes to comply with these newly proposed laws  xB  Read the full article here    For brands looking to boost sustainability within their eCommerce stack   Weve Got Good News and Bad News On the Wave of Regulation Poised to Rock the Fashion Industry

4	The overwhelming amount of information available to new Rolex customers makes familiarizing oneself with the company and selecting a model even more challenging There are currently hundreds of individual references in the Rolex watch catalog each belonging to one of  families  The Catalog of Rolex Classic vs Professional The Classic and Professional models in Rolexs lineup roughly split in half The DayDate Datejust LadyDatejust Oyster Perpetual SkyDweller and Cellini are all examples of Classic watches which are essentially dressier watches that are better suited to daytoday or dressup wear and were not designed specifically for a particular field of work  The Professional watches which include the Air King GMTMaster II YachtMaster Submariner Cosmography Daytona SeaDweller Explorer and Milgauss were all designed specifically for a particular activity such as SCUBA diving yachting driving spelunking or other similar activities  Its important to note that while some Professional watches have more features and are more resistant to water the Classic watches are just as sturdy After all Rolexs SkyDweller one of its most complex watches is in the Classic collectionThe Classic collection includes  Oyster Perpetuals and  SkyDwellers but there is no clear price differentiation between the collections The Professional collection has a similar selection  For more  The Complete Guide to Rolex

4	  How Matthew Jung Founder of The Last Crumb built a luxury cookies brand with the help of Clever Marketing  Consumer Research   Early Work on Building Customer Experiences   Matthew and his cofounder from the beginning knew that their cookies were delicate and highly delicious But from the start they decided to charge people  per cookie and to sell a box of  cookies for  They needed more than a great product   The Cofounder Derek Jaeger knew from the beginning the need for marketing  building better customer experiences to scale the brand   Derek wanted to take the principles used by brands like Rolex Nike and others to anticipate their target customers to forget about the price and think about the experience of eating the cookies   How They Built A Luxury Experience   Derek in one of the interviews said they hadnt spent a dime on marketingHeres How they built a luxury experience with  marketing   Product Packaging The Brand confirms that in the early days they increased the spending on making their Boxes  Cookie packs to ensure consumers love the unboxing experience   Before I get into the next part even though they claimed  marketing spend I indeed think they meant paid marketing   Because they hired Cole Schafer founder of HoneyCopy to help them with Email Marketing  Copywriting    Email Marketing Cole  Cofounder Derek worked on crafting an email marketing strategy The Brand on average hits the customer with more than  emails on your order Explaining the brand story how orders are prepared etc To give the customers that premium experience   The Next part Cole worked on and he mentioned on a podcast that he wanted to visualize the cookies through words with the names of cookies    Product Naming Cole worked on naming the cookies with the usage of clever words and messaging to visualize the cookies to the consumers   With names like What the Fck Velvet Not Today MrMuffin Man  Cent Birthday Cookie Stifflers Mom etc   With every cookie drop They have new names shifting the perspective of buyers on how it will taste based on the name   In Recent Times They have launched newtonew styles of cookies with different names They are anticipating every drop   Using Nikes Sneaker Drop Strategy   The Brand has thousands of people on its waiting lists for cookie drops due to its exclusivity   They use a framework Nike use to drop Sneakers and create exclusivity around the product   The Last Crumb uses the principles of luxury management where they turn cheap products into expensive highdemand products through exclusive distribution strategies like Lottery Drops   Where Selected Customers on a waiting list get the chance to order the product and buy to enjoy the experience   The Reason Exclusive Distribution Strategies work is it doesnt just elevate the customer experience but also help to build the community and provoke Internet discussions   You can find s of Community discussions around their Cookie Drop because Influencers posted they got the drop and people discussed I also tried but bad luck meaning all that exclusivity and a time stamp on getting the cookies created discussions that helped them grow organically faster and better How The Last Crumb Became Luxury Cookies Brand Selling out in less than  Minutes with  Marketing

images all belong in this megathread  xB   Frequently Asked Questions  xB  Who will ship my Steam Deck  xB  In North America USCA this will be FedEx RMAs are also processed by FedEx  xB  In Europe this will be GLS In the UK this will be ParcelForce or EVRI formerly known as Hermes usually in times of industrial action RMAs in Europe are by DHL  In Komodo regions we arent sure yet It will almost certainly be a large local courier service Regardless of who ships it you will receive a tracking number to follow your Decks progress  xB  Update for December  via Valve   xB  Starting December st customers in Japan South Korea Hong Kong and  Taiwan who have already reserved their Steam Deck will receive email  confirmations to finalize their orders These orders will start shipping  on December th  xB  Were happy to announce that Steam Decks will start shipping in Japan  South Korea Hong Kong and Taiwan on December th via Komodo our  official Steam Deck distributor in these regions  Customers in these regions can reserve the Steam Deck here steamdeckkomodojp  xB  Source   xB  Im stuck on Shipping Soon help  xB  Its normal for your order to stay on Shipping Soon for several days We usually see Steam Decks delivered within  working days after placing the order A business day is considered MonFri  xB  If it has been longer than  working days and its still on Shipping Soon you should contact Steam Support for assistance If you have tracking but are past  working days you should await your Steam Deck for longer unless it has been  working days since your last tracking update in which case you should contact Steam Support  xB  My tracking says preadvice  awaiting parcel help  xB  This is a normal step in the process this means your parcel is somewhere between Valves warehouse and your delivery providers first sorting hub Parcels are not scanned until they reach this hub and therefore it can show as preadvice  awaiting parcel even if they do currently have the parcel  xB  This usually changes within  working day though dont be alarmed as it can take up to  working days working days MonFri If its been longer than that you should contact Steam Support  xB  Do FedExGLSParcelForce deliver on Sundays  xB  FedEx delivers to  of the US population on a SundaySundaySunday  xB  In Europe as with most delivery companies GLS  ParcelForce does not typically deliver on a Sunday They may do so in times of peak demand around Christmas but outside of this its unlikely  xB  Both FedEx and GLS do deliver on Saturdays though  xB  UK My parcel is stuck in customs what do I do  xB  This can happen in both the RMA and delivery process but this will usually be sorted and cleared through customs after a short delay In uncommon cases it may take longer on a scale of working days but will still clear  xB  However if at any point the tracking says that additional information is required please contact Steam Support  xB  UK My parcel hasnt updated from the Netherlands in several days should I be concerned  xB  No you should not be concerned This is because there is no tracking update between it leaving the Netherlands Hub and it arriving in the UK for customs checks Depending on several events outside of the control of GLSParcelForce there are many different reasons why this could take a long period of time  xB  My Steam Deck is delayed Im annoyed  xB  Sorry to hear that your Steam Deck has been delayed Unfortunately as with any delivery service its possible for issues and delays to occur during the delivery process  xB  So long as your shipping provider is giving you frequent updates and has not elapsed more than  working days without an update hang tight  xB  If you havent received an update in over  working days MonFri please contact Steam Support  xB  My Steam Deck is brokenstolenlost from delivery help  xB  You should contact Steam Support as soon as possible so that a replacement can be arranged  xB  xB   Shipping Megathread January 4	The overwhelming amount of information available to new Rolex customers makes familiarizing oneself with the company and selecting a model even more challenging There are currently hundreds of individual references in the Rolex watch catalog each belonging to one of  families  The Catalog of Rolex Classic vs Professional The Classic and Professional models in Rolexs lineup roughly split in half The DayDate Datejust LadyDatejust Oyster Perpetual SkyDweller and Cellini are all examples of Classic watches which are essentially dressier watches that are better suited to daytoday or dressup wear and were not designed specifically for a particular field of work  The Professional watches which include the Air King GMTMaster II YachtMaster Submariner Cosmography Daytona SeaDweller Explorer and Milgauss were all designed specifically for a particular activity such as SCUBA diving yachting driving spelunking or other similar activities  Its important to note that while some Professional watches have more features and are more resistant to water the Classic watches are just as sturdy After all Rolexs SkyDweller one of its most complex watches is in the Classic collectionThe Classic collection includes  Oyster Perpetuals and  SkyDwellers but there is no clear price differentiation between the collections The Professional collection has a similar selection  For more  The Complete Guide to Rolex
